<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mascots">Mascots</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Houston_Rockets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Mascots">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Mascot" title="Mascot">mascot</a> of the Houston Rockets in the 1980s was called Booster. From 1993 to 1995, the mascot was Turbo, a costumed man that performed acrobatic dunks and other maneuvers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup> In 1995, the Rockets debuted <a href="/wiki/Clutch_(mascot)" title="Clutch (mascot)">Clutch the Bear</a> as a second mascot, a large teddy bear-like mascot that performs a variety of acts during the games. After eight years of serving as dual mascots, the performer playing Turbo retired, making Clutch the sole mascot for the team.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rivalries">Rivalries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Houston_Rockets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Rivalries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Rockets%E2%80%93Spurs_rivalry" title="Rockets–Spurs rivalry">Rockets–Spurs rivalry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jazz%E2%80%93Rockets_rivalry" title="Jazz–Rockets rivalry">Jazz–Rockets rivalry</a></div>
<p>The Rockets have developed many rivalries within the Western Conference ever since the team returned there in 1980. Two are interstate rivalries, with the San Antonio Spurs, who moved along with the Rockets after four years with them in the Eastern Conference,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup> and the Dallas Mavericks, introduced that very season.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup> Houston faced both Texas teams thrice since 1980, beating the Spurs on all occasions and losing twice to the Mavericks.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> Other famed rivalries were with the <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Lakers" title="Los Angeles Lakers">Los Angeles Lakers</a>, that in the 1980s <a href="/wiki/Showtime_(basketball)" title="Showtime (basketball)">Showtime</a> era only missed the NBA Finals when beaten by the Rockets,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup> and the Utah Jazz, who the Rockets beat in both championship seasons but were defeated by Utah in five other occasions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honors_and_statistics">Honors and statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Houston_Rockets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Honors and statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Retained_draft_rights">Retained draft rights</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Houston_Rockets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Retained draft rights">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Rockets hold the draft rights to the following unsigned draft picks who have been playing outside the NBA. A drafted player, either an international draftee or a college draftee who is not signed by the team that drafted him, is allowed to sign with any non-NBA teams. In this case, the team retains the player's draft rights in the NBA until one year after the player's contract with the non-NBA team ends.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup> This list includes draft rights that were acquired from trades with other teams.</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Unassigned_numbers">Unassigned numbers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Houston_Rockets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Unassigned numbers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul>
<li>11 – <a href="/wiki/Yao_Ming" title="Yao Ming">Yao Ming</a>, <a href="/wiki/Center_(basketball)" title="Center (basketball)">C</a>, (2002–2011). The number has not been issued since Yao announced his retirement on July 20, 2011. Following Yao's recent induction into the Basketball Hall of Fame, it will be retired on February 3, 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180"><a href="#cite_note-180">[180]</a></sup></li>
</ul>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rochester_Royals" title="Rochester Royals">Rochester Royals</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Royals" title="Cincinnati Royals">Cincinnati Royals</a> (1957)</li>

<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philadelphia_Warriors" title="Philadelphia Warriors">Philadelphia Warriors</a>–<a href="/wiki/Golden_State_Warriors" title="Golden State Warriors">San Francisco Warriors</a> (1962)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chicago_Zephyrs" title="Chicago Zephyrs">Chicago Zephyrs</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baltimore_Bullets_(1963%E2%80%931973)" title="Baltimore Bullets (1963–1973)">Baltimore Bullets</a> (1963)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Syracuse_Nationals" title="Syracuse Nationals">Syracuse Nationals</a>–<a href="/wiki/Philadelphia_76ers" title="Philadelphia 76ers">Philadelphia 76ers</a> (1963)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Louis_Hawks" title="St. Louis Hawks">St. Louis Hawks</a>–<a href="/wiki/Atlanta_Hawks" title="Atlanta Hawks">Atlanta Hawks</a> (1968)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego_Rockets" title="San Diego Rockets">San Diego Rockets</a>–<strong class="selflink">Houston Rockets</strong> (1971)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Royals" title="Cincinnati Royals">Cincinnati Royals</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kansas_City%E2%80%93Omaha_Kings" title="Kansas City–Omaha Kings">Kansas City–Omaha Kings</a> (1972)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Baltimore_Bullets_(1963%E2%80%931973)" title="Baltimore Bullets (1963–1973)">Baltimore Bullets</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Capital_Bullets" title="Capital Bullets">Capital Bullets</a> (1973)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kansas_City%E2%80%93Omaha_Kings" title="Kansas City–Omaha Kings">Kansas City–Omaha Kings</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kansas_City_Kings" title="Kansas City Kings">Kansas City Kings</a> (1975)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Buffalo_Braves" title="Buffalo Braves">Buffalo Braves</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego_Clippers" title="San Diego Clippers">San Diego Clippers</a> (1978)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Orleans_Jazz_(NBA_team)" title="New Orleans Jazz (NBA team)">New Orleans Jazz</a>–<a href="/wiki/Utah_Jazz" title="Utah Jazz">Utah Jazz</a> (1979)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/San_Diego_Clippers" title="San Diego Clippers">San Diego Clippers</a>–<a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Clippers" title="Los Angeles Clippers">Los Angeles Clippers</a> (1984)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kansas_City_Kings" title="Kansas City Kings">Kansas City Kings</a>–<a href="/wiki/Sacramento_Kings" title="Sacramento Kings">Sacramento Kings</a> (1985)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vancouver_Grizzlies" title="Vancouver Grizzlies">Vancouver Grizzlies</a>–<a href="/wiki/Memphis_Grizzlies" title="Memphis Grizzlies">Memphis Grizzlies</a> (<a href="/wiki/Vancouver_Grizzlies_relocation_to_Memphis" title="Vancouver Grizzlies relocation to Memphis">2001</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Hornets" title="Charlotte Hornets">Charlotte Hornets</a>–<a href="/wiki/New_Orleans_Pelicans" title="New Orleans Pelicans">New Orleans Hornets</a> (2002)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Orleans_Hornets" title="New Orleans Hornets">New Orleans Hornets</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Orleans/Oklahoma_City_Hornets" title="New Orleans/Oklahoma City Hornets">New Orleans/Oklahoma City Hornets</a> (<a href="/wiki/Effect_of_Hurricane_Katrina_on_the_New_Orleans_Hornets" title="Effect of Hurricane Katrina on the New Orleans Hornets">2005</a>)</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Orleans/Oklahoma_City_Hornets" title="New Orleans/Oklahoma City Hornets">New Orleans/Oklahoma City Hornets</a>–<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Orleans_Hornets" title="New Orleans Hornets">New Orleans Hornets</a> (<a href="/wiki/Effect_of_Hurricane_Katrina_on_the_New_Orleans_Hornets" title="Effect of Hurricane Katrina on the New Orleans Hornets">2007</a>)</li>
